<a name="ADO.NET461" />

### <a name="adonet"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-716">ADO.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-716">ADO.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-717">In ADO.NET è stato aggiunto quanto segue:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-717">The following have been added to ADO.NET:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-718">**Supporto di Crittografia sempre attiva per le chiavi hardware protette**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-718">**Always Encrypted support for hardware protected keys**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-719">ADO.NET ora supporta l'archiviazione nativa delle chiavi master di colonna con Crittografia sempre attiva nei moduli di protezione hardware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-719">ADO.NET now supports storing Always Encrypted column master keys natively in Hardware Security Modules (HSMs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-720">Grazie a questo supporto, i clienti possono usare le chiavi asimmetriche archiviate nei moduli di protezione hardware senza dover scrivere provider dell'archivio chiavi master di colonna personalizzati e senza doverli registrare nelle applicazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-720">With this support, customers can leverage asymmetric keys stored in HSMs without having to write custom column master key store providers and registering them in applications.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-721">I clienti devono installare il provider CSP fornito dal fornitore dei moduli di protezione hardware o i provider dell'archivio chiavi CNG nei server applicazioni o nei computer client per accedere ai dati con Crittografia sempre attiva protetti con le chiavi master di colonna archiviate in un modulo di protezione hardware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-721">Customers need to install the HSM vendor-provided CSP provider or CNG key store providers on the app servers or client computers in order to access Always Encrypted data protected with column master keys stored in a HSM.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-722">**Miglioramento del comportamento di connessione <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.MultiSubnetFailover%2A> per AlwaysOn**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-722">**Improved <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.MultiSubnetFailover%2A> connection behavior for AlwaysOn**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-723">SqlClient ora offre automaticamente connessioni più veloci a un gruppo di disponibilità AlwaysOn.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-723">SqlClient now automatically provides faster connections to an AlwaysOn Availability Group (AG).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-724">Rileva in modo trasparente se l'applicazione si connette a un gruppo di disponibilità AlwaysOn su una subnet diversa e individua rapidamente il server attivo corrente e gli fornisce una connessione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-724">It transparently detects whether your application is connecting to an AlwaysOn availability group (AG) on a different subnet and quickly discovers the current active server and provides a connection to the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-725">Prima di questa versione, un'applicazione doveva impostare la stringa di connessione in modo da includere `"MultisubnetFailover=true"` per indicare che era connessa a un gruppo di disponibilità AlwaysOn.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-725">Prior to this release, an application had to set the connection string to include `"MultisubnetFailover=true"` to indicate that it was connecting to an AlwaysOn Availability Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-726">Senza impostare la parola chiave di connessione su `true`, potrebbe verificarsi un timeout durante la connessione di un'applicazione a un gruppo di disponibilità AlwaysOn.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-726">Without setting the connection keyword to `true`, an application might experience a timeout while connecting to an AlwaysOn Availability Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-727">In questa versione *non* è più necessario che un'applicazione imposti <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.MultiSubnetFailover%2A> su `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-727">With this release, an application does *not* need to set <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.MultiSubnetFailover%2A> to `true` anymore.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-728">Per altre informazioni sul supporto SqlClient per gruppi di disponibilità Always On, vedere [Supporto SqlClient per disponibilità elevata, ripristino di emergenza](../data/adonet/sql/sqlclient-support-for-high-availability-disaster-recovery.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-728">For more information about SqlClient support for Always On Availability Groups, see [SqlClient Support for High Availability, Disaster Recovery](../data/adonet/sql/sqlclient-support-for-high-availability-disaster-recovery.md).</span></span>

<a name="WPF461" />

### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-729">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-729">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-730">Windows Presentation Foundation include molti miglioramenti e cambiamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-730">Windows Presentation Foundation includes a number of improvements and changes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-731">**Miglioramento delle prestazioni**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-731">**Improved performance**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-732">Il ritardo di attivazione degli eventi tocco è stato risolto in .NET Framework 4.6.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-732">The delay in firing touch events has been fixed in the .NET Framework 4.6.1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-733">Inoltre, l'inserimento di un controllo <xref:System.Windows.Controls.RichTextBox> non blocca più il thread di rendering durante l'input veloce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-733">In addition, typing in a <xref:System.Windows.Controls.RichTextBox> control no longer ties up the render thread during fast input.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-734">**Miglioramenti di controllo ortografico**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-734">**Spell checking improvements**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-735">Il controllo ortografico in WPF è stato aggiornato in Windows 8.1 e versioni successive per sfruttare il supporto di altre lingue per il controllo ortografico offerto dal sistema operativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-735">The spell checker in WPF has been updated on Windows 8.1 and later versions to leverage operating system support for spell-checking additional languages.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-736">La funzionalità non è stata modificata nelle versioni di Windows precedenti a Windows 8.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-736">There is no change in functionality on Windows versions prior to Windows 8.1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-737">Come nelle versioni precedenti di .NET Framework, la lingua per un controllo <xref:System.Windows.Controls.TextBox> o un blocco <xref:System.Windows.Controls.RichTextBox> viene rilevata cercando le informazioni nell'ordine seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-737">As in previous versions of the .NET Framework, the language for a <xref:System.Windows.Controls.TextBox> control ora <xref:System.Windows.Controls.RichTextBox> block is detected by looking for information in the following order:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-738">`xml:lang`, se presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-738">`xml:lang`, if it is present.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-739">Lingua di input corrente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-739">Current input language.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-740">Impostazioni cultura del thread corrente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-740">Current thread culture.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-741">Per altre informazioni sul supporto delle lingue in WPF, vedere il [post di blog di WPF sulle funzionalità di .NET Framework 4.6.1](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/wpf/wpf-in-net-4-6-1/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-741">For additional information on language support in WPF, see the [WPF blog post on .NET Framework 4.6.1 features](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/wpf/wpf-in-net-4-6-1/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-742">**Supporto aggiuntivo per i dizionari personalizzati per utente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-742">**Additional support for per-user custom dictionaries**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-743">In .NET Framework 4.6.1, WPF riconosce i dizionari personalizzati che sono registrati a livello globale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-743">In .NET Framework 4.6.1, WPF recognizes custom dictionaries that are registered globally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-744">Questa funzionalità si aggiunge alla possibilità di registrarli a livello di controllo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-744">This capability is available in addition to the ability to register them per-control.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-745">Nelle versioni precedenti di WPF, i dizionari personalizzati non riconoscono le parole escluse e gli elenchi di correzione automatica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-745">In previous versions of WPF, custom dictionaries did not recognize Excluded Words and AutoCorrect lists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-746">Sono supportati in Windows 8.1 e Windows 10 mediante l'uso di file che possono essere inseriti nella directory `%AppData%\Microsoft\Spelling\<language tag>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-746">They are supported on Windows 8.1 and Windows 10 through the use of files that can be placed under the `%AppData%\Microsoft\Spelling\<language tag>` directory.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-747">A questi file si applicano le regole seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-747">The following rules apply to these files:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-748">I file devono avere estensione dic (per le parole aggiunte), exc (per le parole escluse) o acl (per la correzione automatica).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-748">The files should have extensions of .dic (for added words), .exc (for excluded words), or .acl (for AutoCorrect).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-749">I file devono essere in testo normale UTF-16 LE che inizia con l'indicatore dell'ordine dei byte (BOM, Byte Order Mark).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-749">The files should be UTF-16 LE plaintext that starts with the Byte Order Mark (BOM).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-750">Ogni riga deve essere costituita da una parola, negli elenchi di parole aggiunte ed escluse, o da una coppia della correzione automatica con le parole separate da una barra verticale ("&#124;"), nell'elenco di parole della correzione automatica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-750">Each line should consist of a word (in the added and excluded word lists), or an autocorrect pair with the words separated by a vertical bar ("&#124;") (in the AutoCorrect word list).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-751">Questi file sono considerati di sola lettura e non vengono modificati dal sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-751">These files are considered read-only and are not modified by the system.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-752">Questi nuovi formati di file non sono supportati direttamente dalle API di controllo ortografico WPF e i dizionari personalizzati forniti a WPF nelle applicazioni devono continuare a usare i file con estensione lex.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-752">These new file-formats are not directly supported by the WPF spell checking APIs, and the custom dictionaries supplied to WPF in applications should continue to use .lex files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-753">**Esempi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-753">**Samples**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-754">Sono disponibili numerosi esempi di WPF nel repository GitHub [Microsoft/WPF-Samples](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPF-Samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-754">There are a number of WPF samples on the [Microsoft/WPF-Samples](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPF-Samples) GitHub repository.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-755">Per aiutare Microsoft a migliorare gli esempi, inviare una richiesta di pull o segnalare un [problema di GitHub](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPF-Samples/issues).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-755">Help us improve our samples by sending us a pull-request or opening a [GitHub issue](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPF-Samples/issues).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-756">**Estensioni DirectX**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-756">**DirectX extensions**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-757">WPF include un [pacchetto NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.Wpf.Interop.DirectX-x86/) che offre nuove implementazioni di <xref:System.Windows.Interop.D3DImage>, le quali semplificano l'interazione con il contenuto DX10 e Dx11.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-757">WPF includes a [NuGet package](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.Wpf.Interop.DirectX-x86/) that provides new implementations of <xref:System.Windows.Interop.D3DImage> that make it easy for you to interoperate with DX10 and Dx11 content.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-758">Il codice per questo pacchetto è stato reso open source ed è disponibile su [GitHub](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPFDXInterop).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-758">The code for this package has been open sourced and is available [on GitHub](https://github.com/Microsoft/WPFDXInterop).</span></span>

<a name="WWF461" />

### <a name="windows-workflow-foundation-transactions"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-759">Windows Workflow Foundation: Transazioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-759">Windows Workflow Foundation: Transactions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-760">Il metodo <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> ora può usare un gestore di transazioni distribuite diverso da MSDTC per alzare di livello la transazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-760">The <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method can now use a distributed transaction manager other than MSDTC to promote the transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-761">A questo scopo, specificare un identificatore del promotore della transazione GUID nel nuovo overload <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%28System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification%2CSystem.Guid%29?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-761">You do this by specifying a GUID transaction promoter identifier to the  new <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%28System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification%2CSystem.Guid%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> overload .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-762">Se l'operazione riesce, le funzionalità della transazione sono soggette a limitazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-762">If this operation is successful, there are limitations placed on the capabilities of the transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-763">Quando viene integrato un promotore di transazione non MSDTC, i metodi seguenti generano un'eccezione <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionPromotionException> perché questi metodi richiedono l'innalzamento di livello a MSDTC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-763">Once a non-MSDTC transaction promoter is enlisted, the following methods throw a <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionPromotionException> because these methods require promotion to MSDTC:</span></span>

- <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

- <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionInterop.GetDtcTransaction%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

- <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionInterop.GetExportCookie%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

- <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionInterop.GetTransmitterPropagationToken%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-764">Quando viene integrato un promotore di transazione non MSDTC, occorre usarlo per le future integrazioni durevoli usando i protocolli che definisce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-764">Once a non-MSDTC transaction promoter is enlisted, it must be used for future durable enlistments by using protocols that it defines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-765">L'oggetto <xref:System.Guid> del promotore di transazione può essere ottenuto mediante la proprietà <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoterType%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-765">The <xref:System.Guid> of the transaction promoter can be obtained by using the <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoterType%2A> property.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-766">Quando la transazione viene alzata di livello, il promotore di transazione fornisce una matrice <xref:System.Byte> che rappresenta il token alzato di livello.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-766">When the transaction promotes, the transaction promoter provides a <xref:System.Byte> array that represents the promoted token.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-767">Un'applicazione può ottenere il token alzato di livello per una transazione non MSDTC alzata di livello con il metodo <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.GetPromotedToken%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-767">An application can obtain the promoted token for a non-MSDTC promoted transaction with the <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.GetPromotedToken%2A> method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-768">Gli utenti del nuovo overload <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%28System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification%2CSystem.Guid%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> devono seguire una specifica sequenza di chiamate affinché l'operazione di promozione venga completata correttamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-768">Users of the new <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%28System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification%2CSystem.Guid%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> overload must follow a specific call sequence in order for the promotion operation to complete successfully.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-769">Queste regole sono descritte nella documentazione relativa al metodo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-769">These rules are documented in the method's documentation.</span></span>

<a name="Profile461" />

### <a name="profiling"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-770">Profilatura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-770">Profiling</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-771">L'API di profilatura non gestita è stata migliorata nel modo seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-771">The unmanaged profiling API has been enhanced as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-772">Supporto migliorato per l'accesso ai PDB nell'interfaccia [ICorProfilerInfo7](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-interface.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-772">Better support for accessing PDBs in the [ICorProfilerInfo7](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-interface.md) interface.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-773">In ASP.NET Core è sempre più comune che gli assembly vengano compilati in memoria mediante Roslyn.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-773">In ASP.NET Core, it is becoming much more common for assemblies to be compiled in-memory by Roslyn.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-774">Per gli sviluppatori che creano strumenti di profilatura, ciò significa che i PDB che in passato erano serializzati sul disco potrebbero non essere più presenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-774">For developers making profiling tools, this means that PDBs that historically were serialized on disk may no longer be present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-775">Gli strumenti profiler spesso usano PDB per rimappare il codice alle righe di origine per attività come il code coverage o l'analisi delle prestazioni riga per riga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-775">Profiler tools often use PDBs to map code back to source lines for tasks such as code coverage or line-by-line performance analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-776">L'interfaccia [ICorProfilerInfo7](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-interface.md) include ora due nuovi metodi, [ICorProfilerInfo7::GetInMemorySymbolsLength](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-getinmemorysymbolslength-method.md) e [ICorProfilerInfo7::ReadInMemorySymbols](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-readinmemorysymbols.md), per fornire a questi strumenti profiler l'accesso ai dati dei PDB in memoria. Usando le nuove API, un profiler può ottenere il contenuto di un PDB in memoria come matrice di byte e quindi elaborarlo o serializzarlo su disco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-776">The [ICorProfilerInfo7](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-interface.md) interface now includes two new methods, [ICorProfilerInfo7::GetInMemorySymbolsLength](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-getinmemorysymbolslength-method.md) and [ICorProfilerInfo7::ReadInMemorySymbols](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-readinmemorysymbols.md), to provide these profiler tools with access to the in-memory PDB data, By using the new APIs, a profiler can obtain the contents of an in-memory PDB as a byte array and then process it or serialize it to disk.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-777">Strumentazione migliore con l'interfaccia ICorProfiler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-777">Better instrumentation with the ICorProfiler interface.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-778">I profiler che usano la funzionalità ReJit dell'API `ICorProfiler` per la strumentazione dinamica ora possono modificare alcuni metadati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-778">Profilers that are using the `ICorProfiler` APIs ReJit functionality for dynamic instrumentation can now modify some metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-779">In precedenza quegli strumenti potevano instrumentare IL in qualsiasi momento, ma i metadati potevano essere modificati solo in fase di caricamento del modulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-779">Previously such tools could instrument IL at any time, but metadata could only be modified at module load time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-780">Poiché IL fa riferimento ai metadati, questo limitava i tipi di strumentazione possibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-780">Because IL refers to metadata, this limited the kinds of instrumentation that could be done.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-781">Alcuni di questi limiti sono stati innalzati aggiungendo il metodo [ICorProfilerInfo7::ApplyMetaData](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-applymetadata-method.md) per supportare un subset di modifiche ai metadati dopo il caricamento del modulo, in particolare aggiungendo nuovi record `AssemblyRef`, `TypeRef`, `TypeSpec`, `MemberRef`, `MemberSpec` e `UserString`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-781">We have lifted some of those limits by adding the [ICorProfilerInfo7::ApplyMetaData](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo7-applymetadata-method.md) method to support a subset of metadata edits after the module loads, in particular by adding new `AssemblyRef`, `TypeRef`, `TypeSpec`, `MemberRef`, `MemberSpec`, and `UserString` records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-782">Questa modifica rende possibile una gamma più ampia di strumentazioni immediate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-782">This change makes a much broader range of on-the-fly instrumentation possible.</span></span>

<a name="NGEN461" />

### <a name="native-image-generator-ngen-pdbs"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-783">PDB del generatore di immagini native (NGEN)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-783">Native Image Generator (NGEN) PDBs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-784">La traccia eventi tra computer consente ai clienti di profilare un programma sul Computer A e osservare i dati di profilatura con mapping della riga di origine sul Computer B. Nelle versioni precedenti di .NET Framework, l'utente copiava tutti i moduli e le immagini native dalla macchina profilata alla macchina di analisi contenente il PDB IL per creare il mapping sorgente-nativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-784">Cross-machine event tracing allows customers to profile a program on Machine A and look at the profiling data with source line mapping on Machine B. Using previous versions of the .NET Framework, the user would copy all the modules and native images from the profiled machine to the analysis machine that contains the IL PDB to create the source-to-native mapping.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-785">Anche se questo processo può funzionare bene quando i file sono relativamente piccoli, ad esempio per le applicazioni telefoniche, i file possono avere dimensioni molto grandi sui sistemi desktop e la copia può richiedere molto tempo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-785">While this process may work well when the files are relatively small, such as for phone applications, the files can be very large on desktop systems and require significant time to copy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-786">Con i PDB Ngen, NGen può creare un PDB che contiene il mapping da IL a nativo senza una dipendenza dal PDB IL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-786">With Ngen PDBs, NGen can create a PDB that contains the IL-to-native mapping without a dependency on the IL PDB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-787">In questo scenario di traccia eventi in più computer, è sufficiente copiare il PDB di immagine nativa generato dal Computer A nel Computer B e usare le [API di accesso all'interfaccia di debug](/visualstudio/debugger/debug-interface-access/debug-interface-access-sdk-reference) per leggere il mapping da codice sorgente a codice IL del PDB IL e il mapping da codice IL a codice nativo del PDB di immagine nativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-787">In our cross-machine event tracing scenario, all that is needed is to copy the native image PDB that is generated by Machine A to Machine B and to use [Debug Interface Access APIs](/visualstudio/debugger/debug-interface-access/debug-interface-access-sdk-reference) to read the IL PDB's source-to-IL mapping and the native image PDB's IL-to-native mapping.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-788">La combinazione di entrambi i mapping fornisce un mapping da codice sorgente a codice nativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-788">Combining both mappings provides a source-to-native mapping.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-789">Poiché il PDB di immagine nativa è molto più piccolo rispetto a tutti i moduli e alle immagini native, il processo di copia dal Computer A al Computer B è molto più veloce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-789">Since the native image PDB is much smaller than all the modules and native images, the process of copying from Machine A to Machine B is much faster.</span></span>

<a name="v46" />

## <a name="whats-new-in-net-2015"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-790">Novità di .NET 2015</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-790">What's new in .NET 2015</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-791">.NET 2015 introduce .NET Framework 4.6 e .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-791">.NET 2015 introduces the .NET Framework 4.6 and .NET Core.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-792">Alcune nuove funzionalità sono valide per entrambi, mentre altre sono specifiche di .NET Framework 4.6 o .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-792">Some new features apply to both, and other features are specific to .NET Framework 4.6 or .NET Core.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-793">**ASP.NET Core**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-793">**ASP.NET Core**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-794">.NET 2015 include ASP.NET Core, un'implementazione di .NET snella per lo sviluppo di app moderne basate su cloud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-794">.NET 2015 includes ASP.NET Core, which is a lean .NET implementation for building modern cloud-based apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-795">ASP.NET Core è modulare e consente quindi di includere solo le funzionalità necessarie nell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-795">ASP.NET Core is modular so you can include only those features that are needed in your application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-796">Può essere ospitata su IIS o in modo indipendente in un processo personalizzato ed è possibile eseguire app con diverse versioni di .NET Framework nello stesso server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-796">It can be hosted on IIS or self-hosted in a custom process, and you can run apps with different versions of the .NET Framework on the same server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-797">Include un nuovo sistema di configurazione dell'ambiente progettato per la distribuzione cloud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-797">It includes a new environment configuration system that is designed for cloud deployment.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-798">MVC, API Web e pagine Web sono riunite in un unico framework denominato MVC 6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-798">MVC, Web API, and Web Pages are unified into a single framework called MVC 6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-799">Le app ASP.NET Core vengono compilate mediante gli strumenti in Visual Studio 2015 o versione successiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-799">You build ASP.NET Core apps through tools in Visual Studio 2015 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-800">Le applicazioni esistenti funzioneranno nel nuovo .NET Framework ma per compilare un'app che usa MVC 6 o SignalR 3 è necessario usare il sistema di progetto in Visual Studio 2015 o versione successiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-800">Your existing applications will work on the new .NET Framework; however to build an app that uses MVC 6 or SignalR 3, you must use the project system in Visual Studio 2015 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-801">Per informazioni, vedere [ASP.NET Core](/aspnet/core/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-801">For information, see [ASP.NET Core](/aspnet/core/).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-802">**Aggiornamenti di ASP.NET**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-802">**ASP.NET Updates**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-803">**API basata su attività per lo scaricamento asincrono delle risposte**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-803">**Task-based API for Asynchronous Response Flushing**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-804">ASP.NET ora fornisce <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.FlushAsync%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, una semplice API basata sulle attività che consente di scaricare le risposte asincrone con il supporto `async/await` del linguaggio usato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-804">ASP.NET now provides a simple task-based API for asynchronous response flushing, <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.FlushAsync%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, that allows responses to be flushed asynchronously by using your language's `async/await` support.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-805">**L'associazione di modelli supporta i metodi che restituiscono attività**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-805">**Model binding supports task-returning methods**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-806">In .NET Framework 4.5, ASP.NET ha aggiunto la funzionalità di associazione di modelli che ha reso possibile un approccio estendibile, focalizzato sul codice, per le operazioni di dati basate su CRUD nelle pagine Web Form e nei controlli utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-806">In the .NET Framework 4.5, ASP.NET added the Model Binding feature that enabled an extensible, code-focused approach to CRUD-based data operations in Web Forms pages and user controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-807">Il sistema di associazione di modelli ora supporta metodi di associazione di modelli con restituzione di <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-807">The Model Binding system now supports <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task>-returning model binding methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-808">Questa funzionalità consente agli sviluppatori di Web Form di ottenere i vantaggi di scalabilità di async con la facilità del sistema di associazione dati quando usano versioni più recenti di ORM, tra cui Entity Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-808">This feature allows Web Forms developers to get the scalability benefits of async with the ease of the data-binding system when using newer versions of ORMs, including the Entity Framework.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-809">L'associazione di modelli async è controllata dall'impostazione di configurazione `aspnet:EnableAsyncModelBinding`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-809">Async model binding is controlled by the `aspnet:EnableAsyncModelBinding` configuration setting.</span></span>

    ```xml
    <appSettings>
        <add key=" aspnet:EnableAsyncModelBinding" value="true|false" />
    </appSettings>
    ```

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-810">Per le app destinate a .NET Framework 4.6, l'impostazione predefinita è `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-810">On apps the target the .NET Framework 4.6, it defaults to `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-811">Per le app in esecuzione su .NET Framework 4.6 e che sono destinate a una versione precedente di .NET Framework, è `false` per impostazione predefinita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-811">On apps running on the .NET Framework 4.6 that target an earlier version of the .NET Framework, it is `false` by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-812">Può essere abilitata impostando l'impostazione di configurazione su `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-812">It can be enabled by setting the configuration setting to `true`.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-813">**Supporto HTTP/2 (Windows 10)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-813">**HTTP/2 Support (Windows 10)**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-814">[HTTP/2](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP/2) è una nuova versione del protocollo HTTP che permette un utilizzo molto migliore della connessione, con meno round trip tra client e server, offrendo una latenza minore per il caricamento delle pagine Web per gli utenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-814">[HTTP/2](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP/2) is a new version of the HTTP protocol that provides much better connection utilization (fewer round-trips between client and server), resulting in lower latency web page loading for users.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-815">Le pagine Web (a differenza dei servizi) traggono maggiori vantaggi dal protocollo HTTP/2, poiché ottimizza più elementi richiesti come parte di un'esperienza unica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-815">Web pages (as opposed to services) benefit the most from HTTP/2, since the protocol optimizes for multiple artifacts being requested as part of a single experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-816">Il supporto HTTP/2 è stato aggiunto ad ASP.NET in .NET Framework 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-816">HTTP/2 support has been added to ASP.NET in .NET Framework 4.6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-817">Poiché la funzionalità di rete esiste a più livelli, si sono rese necessarie nuove funzionalità in Windows, IIS e ASP.NET per abilitare HTTP/2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-817">Because networking functionality exists at multiple layers, new features were required in Windows, in IIS, and in ASP.NET to enable HTTP/2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-818">È necessario eseguire Windows 10 per usare HTTP/2 con ASP.NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-818">You must be running on Windows 10 to use HTTP/2 with ASP.NET.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-819">HTTP/2 è anche supportato e attivato per impostazione predefinita per le app di Windows 10 Universal Windows Platform (UWP) che usano l'API <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClient?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-819">HTTP/2 is also supported and on by default for Windows 10 Universal Windows Platform (UWP) apps that use the <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClient?displayProperty=nameWithType> API.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-820">Per consentire l'uso della funzionalità [PUSH_PROMISE](https://http2.github.io/http2-spec/#PUSH_PROMISE) nelle applicazioni ASP.NET, è stato aggiunto un nuovo metodo con due overload, <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.PushPromise%28System.String%29> e <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.PushPromise%28System.String%2CSystem.String%2CSystem.Collections.Specialized.NameValueCollection%29>, alla classe <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-820">In order to provide a way to use the [PUSH_PROMISE](https://http2.github.io/http2-spec/#PUSH_PROMISE) feature in ASP.NET applications, a new method with two overloads, <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.PushPromise%28System.String%29> and <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.PushPromise%28System.String%2CSystem.String%2CSystem.Collections.Specialized.NameValueCollection%29>, has been added to the <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse> class.</span></span>

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="80feb-821">Mentre ASP.NET Core supporta HTTP/2, il supporto della funzionalità PUSH PROMISE non è ancora stato aggiunto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-821">While ASP.NET Core supports HTTP/2, support for the PUSH PROMISE feature has not yet been added.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-822">Il browser e il server Web (IIS su Windows) eseguono tutte le operazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-822">The browser and the web server (IIS on Windows) do all the work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-823">Gli utenti non dovranno eseguire alcuna operazione impegnativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-823">You don't have to do any heavy-lifting for your users.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-824">Poiché la maggior parte dei [principali browser supporta HTTP/2](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP/2), è probabile che gli utenti trarranno vantaggio dal supporto HTTP/2, se supportato dal server in uso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-824">Most of the [major browsers support HTTP/2](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP/2), so it's likely that your users will benefit from HTTP/2 support if your server supports it.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-825">**Supporto per Token Binding Protocol**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-825">**Support for the Token Binding Protocol**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-826">Microsoft e Google stanno collaborando a un nuovo approccio all'autenticazione, chiamato [Token Binding Protocol](https://github.com/TokenBinding/Internet-Drafts).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-826">Microsoft and Google have been collaborating on a new approach to authentication, called the [Token Binding Protocol](https://github.com/TokenBinding/Internet-Drafts).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-827">Il presupposto è che i token di autenticazione (nella cache del browser) possono essere rubati e usati da utenti malintenzionati per accedere a risorse altrimenti sicure, ad esempio un conto bancario, senza richiedere la password o altre informazioni riservate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-827">The premise is that authentication tokens (in your browser cache) can be stolen and used by criminals to access otherwise secure resources (e.g. your bank account) without requiring your password or any other privileged knowledge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-828">L'obiettivo del nuovo protocollo è attenuare questo problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-828">The new protocol aims to mitigate this problem.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-829">Il Token Binding Protocol verrà implementato in Windows 10 come funzionalità del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-829">The Token Binding Protocol will be implemented in Windows 10 as a browser feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-830">Le app ASP.NET parteciperanno al protocollo, in modo che sia convalidata la legittimità dei token di autenticazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-830">ASP.NET apps will participate in the protocol, so that authentication tokens are validated to be legitimate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-831">Le implementazioni di client e server stabiliscono la protezione end-to-end specificata dal protocollo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-831">The client and the server implementations establish the end-to-end protection specified by the protocol.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-832">**Algoritmi hash casuali per le stringhe**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-832">**Randomized string hash algorithms**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-833">In .NET Framework 4.5 è stato introdotto un [algoritmo hash casuale per le stringhe](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-833">.NET Framework 4.5 introduced a [randomized string hash algorithm](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-834">Tuttavia, non era supportato da ASP.NET perché alcune funzionalità ASP.NET dipendevano da un codice hash stabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-834">However, it was not supported by ASP.NET because of some ASP.NET features depended on a stable hash code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-835">In .NET Framework 4.6 gli algoritmi di hash della stringa casuale sono ora supportati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-835">In .NET Framework 4.6, randomized string hash algorithms are now supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-836">Per abilitare questa funzionalità, usare l'impostazione di configurazione `aspnet:UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-836">To enable this feature, use the `aspnet:UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm` config setting.</span></span>

    ```xml
    <appSettings>
        <add key="aspnet:UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm" value="true|false" />
    </appSettings>
    ```

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-837">**ADO.NET**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-837">**ADO.NET**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-838">ADO .NET supporta ora la funzionalità Crittografia sempre attiva disponibile in SQL Server 2016 Community Technology Preview 2 (CTP2).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-838">ADO .NET now supports the Always Encrypted feature available in SQL Server 2016 Community Technology Preview 2 (CTP2).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-839">Con Crittografia sempre attiva, SQL Server può eseguire operazioni su dati crittografati e, soprattutto, la chiave di crittografia risiede con l'applicazione all'interno dell'ambiente attendibile del cliente e non sul server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-839">With Always Encrypted, SQL Server can perform operations on encrypted data, and best of all the encryption key resides with the application inside the customer’s trusted environment and not on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-840">Crittografia sempre attiva protegge i dati dei clienti in modo che gli amministratori di database non abbiano accesso ai dati di testo normale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-840">Always Encrypted secures customer data so DBAs do not have access to plain text data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-841">La crittografia e la decrittografia dei dati avvengono in modo trasparente a livello di driver, riducendo al minimo le modifiche che è necessario apportare alle applicazioni esistenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-841">Encryption and decryption of data happens transparently at the driver level, minimizing changes that have to be made to existing applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-842">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere [Crittografia sempre attiva (motore di database)](/sql/relational-databases/security/encryption/always-encrypted-database-engine) e [Crittografia sempre attiva (sviluppo client)](/sql/relational-databases/security/encryption/always-encrypted-client-development).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-842">For details, see [Always Encrypted (Database Engine)](/sql/relational-databases/security/encryption/always-encrypted-database-engine) and [Always Encrypted (client development)](/sql/relational-databases/security/encryption/always-encrypted-client-development).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-843">**Compilatore JIT a 64 bit per il codice gestito**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-843">**64-bit JIT Compiler for managed code**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-844">.NET Framework 4.6 presenta una nuova versione del compilatore JIT a 64 bit (il cui nome in codice iniziale è RyuJIT).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-844">.NET Framework 4.6 features a new version of the 64-bit JIT compiler (originally code-named RyuJIT).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-845">Il nuovo compilatore a 64 bit offre miglioramenti significativi delle prestazioni rispetto al compilatore JIT a 64 bit esistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-845">The new 64-bit compiler provides significant performance improvements over the older 64-bit JIT compiler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-846">Il nuovo compilatore a 64 bit è abilitato per i processi a 64 bit in esecuzione su NET Framework 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-846">The new 64-bit compiler is enabled for 64-bit processes running on top of .NET Framework 4.6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-847">L'app verrà eseguita in un processo a 64 bit se è compilata come 64 bit o AnyCPU e se viene eseguita su un sistema operativo a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-847">Your app will run in a 64-bit process if it is compiled as 64-bit or AnyCPU and is running on a 64-bit operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-848">Nonostante si sia cercato di rendere il più possibile trasparente la transizione al nuovo compilatore, potrebbero verificarsi cambiamenti del comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-848">While care has been taken to make the transition to the new compiler as transparent as possible, changes in behavior are possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-849">Microsoft è interessata a conoscere i commenti diretti degli utenti sugli eventuali problemi riscontrati durante l'uso del nuovo compilatore JIT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-849">We would like to hear directly about any issues encountered when using the new JIT compiler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-850">In caso di problemi che potrebbero essere correlati al nuovo compilatore JIT a 64 bit, contattare Microsoft tramite [Microsoft Connect](https://connect.microsoft.com/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-850">Please contact us through [Microsoft Connect](https://connect.microsoft.com/) if you encounter an issue that may be related to the new 64-bit JIT compiler.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-851">Il nuovo compilatore JIT a 64 bit include anche funzionalità di accelerazione SIMD hardware quando è associato a tipi abilitati per SIMD nello spazio dei nomi <xref:System.Numerics>, con conseguente ottimizzazione delle prestazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-851">The new 64-bit JIT compiler also includes hardware SIMD acceleration features when coupled with SIMD-enabled types in the <xref:System.Numerics> namespace, which can yield good performance improvements.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-852">**Miglioramenti apportati al caricatore di assembly**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-852">**Assembly loader improvements**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-853">Il caricatore di assembly usa la memoria in modo più efficiente scaricando gli assembly IL dopo il caricamento di un'immagine NGEN corrispondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-853">The assembly loader now uses memory more efficiently by unloading IL assemblies after a corresponding NGEN image is loaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-854">Questa modifica riduce la memoria virtuale, aspetto particolarmente utile per app a 32 bit di grandi dimensioni (ad esempio Visual Studio) e consente anche di risparmiare memoria fisica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-854">This change decreases virtual memory, which is particularly beneficial for large 32-bit apps (such as Visual Studio), and also saves physical memory.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-855">**Modifiche apportate alla libreria di classi base**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-855">**Base class library changes**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-856">Sono state aggiunte molte nuove API a .NET Framework 4.6 per abilitare gli scenari principali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-856">Many new APIs have been added around to .NET Framework 4.6 to enable key scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-857">Sono incluse le modifiche e le aggiunte seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-857">These include the following changes and additions:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-858">Implementazioni **IReadOnlyCollection\<T>**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-858">**IReadOnlyCollection\<T> implementations**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-859">Altre raccolte implementano <xref:System.Collections.Generic.IReadOnlyCollection%601>, ad esempio <xref:System.Collections.Generic.Queue%601> e <xref:System.Collections.Generic.Stack%601>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-859">Additional collections implement <xref:System.Collections.Generic.IReadOnlyCollection%601> such as <xref:System.Collections.Generic.Queue%601> and <xref:System.Collections.Generic.Stack%601>.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-860">**CultureInfo.CurrentCulture e CultureInfo.CurrentUICulture**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-860">**CultureInfo.CurrentCulture and CultureInfo.CurrentUICulture**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-861">Le proprietà <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> e <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentUICulture%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> ora sono di lettura/scrittura anziché di sola lettura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-861">The <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentCulture%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo.CurrentUICulture%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> properties are now read-write rather than read-only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-862">Se si assegna un nuovo oggetto <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> a queste proprietà, cambiano anche le impostazioni cultura del thread corrente definite dalla proprietà `Thread.CurrentThread.CurrentCulture` e le impostazioni cultura del thread UI corrente definite dalle proprietà `Thread.CurrentThread.CurrentUICulture`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-862">If you assign a new <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> object to these properties, the current thread culture defined by the `Thread.CurrentThread.CurrentCulture` property and the current UI thread culture defined by the `Thread.CurrentThread.CurrentUICulture` properties also change.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-863">**Miglioramenti apportati a Garbage Collection (GC)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-863">**Enhancements to garbage collection (GC)**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-864">La classe <xref:System.GC> ora include i metodi <xref:System.GC.TryStartNoGCRegion%2A> e <xref:System.GC.EndNoGCRegion%2A> che consentono di disabilitare le operazioni di Garbage Collection durante l'esecuzione di un percorso critico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-864">The <xref:System.GC> class now includes <xref:System.GC.TryStartNoGCRegion%2A> and <xref:System.GC.EndNoGCRegion%2A> methods that allow you to disallow garbage collection during the execution of a critical path.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-865">Un nuovo overload del metodo <xref:System.GC.Collect%28System.Int32%2CSystem.GCCollectionMode%2CSystem.Boolean%2CSystem.Boolean%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> consente di controllare se l'heap oggetti piccoli e l'heap oggetti grandi vengono entrambi sottoposti a sweep e compattati o solo sottoposti a sweep.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-865">A new overload of the <xref:System.GC.Collect%28System.Int32%2CSystem.GCCollectionMode%2CSystem.Boolean%2CSystem.Boolean%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> method allows you to control whether both the small object heap and the large object heap are swept and compacted or swept only.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-866">**Tipi abilitati per SIMD**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-866">**SIMD-enabled types**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-867">Lo spazio dei nomi <xref:System.Numerics> ora include numerosi tipi abilitati per SIMD, ad esempio <xref:System.Numerics.Matrix3x2>, <xref:System.Numerics.Matrix4x4>, <xref:System.Numerics.Plane>, <xref:System.Numerics.Quaternion>, <xref:System.Numerics.Vector2>, <xref:System.Numerics.Vector3> e <xref:System.Numerics.Vector4>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-867">The <xref:System.Numerics> namespace now includes a number of SIMD-enabled types, such as <xref:System.Numerics.Matrix3x2>, <xref:System.Numerics.Matrix4x4>, <xref:System.Numerics.Plane>, <xref:System.Numerics.Quaternion>, <xref:System.Numerics.Vector2>, <xref:System.Numerics.Vector3>, and <xref:System.Numerics.Vector4>.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-868">Il nuovo compilatore JIT a 64 bit include anche funzionalità di accelerazione SIMD hardware, quindi le prestazioni migliorano notevolmente quando si usano i tipi abilitati per SIMD con il nuovo compilatore JIT a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-868">Because the new 64-bit JIT compiler also includes hardware SIMD acceleration features, there are especially significant performance improvements when using the SIMD-enabled types with the new 64-bit JIT compiler.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-869">**Aggiornamenti della crittografia**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-869">**Cryptography updates**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-870">L'API <xref:System.Security.Cryptography?displayProperty=nameWithType> è in fase di aggiornamento per supportare le [API di crittografia CNG di Windows](/windows/desktop/SecCNG/cng-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-870">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography?displayProperty=nameWithType> API is being updated to support the [Windows CNG cryptography APIs](/windows/desktop/SecCNG/cng-reference).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-871">Le versioni precedenti di .NET Framework si basavano interamente su una [versione precedente delle API di crittografia Windows](/windows/desktop/SecCrypto/cryptography-portal) per l'implementazione di <xref:System.Security.Cryptography?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-871">Previous versions of the .NET Framework have relied entirely on an [earlier version of the Windows Cryptography APIs](/windows/desktop/SecCrypto/cryptography-portal) as the basis for the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography?displayProperty=nameWithType> implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-872">Microsoft ha ricevuto alcune richieste relative all'aggiunta del supporto per l'API CNG, perché questa supporta [algoritmi di crittografia moderni](/windows/desktop/SecCNG/cng-features#suite-b-support), che sono importanti per determinate categorie di app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-872">We have had requests to support the CNG API, since it supports [modern cryptography algorithms](/windows/desktop/SecCNG/cng-features#suite-b-support), which are important for certain categories of apps.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-873">.NET Framework 4.6 include i nuovi miglioramenti seguenti per supportare le API di crittografia di CNG di Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-873">.NET Framework 4.6 includes the following new enhancements to support the Windows CNG cryptography APIs:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-874">Un set di metodi di estensione per certificati X509, `System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPublicKey(System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2)` e `System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey(System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2)`, che restituiscono, quando possibile, un'implementazione basata su CNG invece di un'implementazione basata su CAPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-874">A set of extension methods for X509 Certificates, `System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPublicKey(System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2)` and `System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey(System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2)`, that return a CNG-based implementation rather than a CAPI-based implementation when possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-875">Ad esempio, alcune smart card richiedono comunque CAPI e le API gestiscono il fallback.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-875">(Some smartcards, etc., still require CAPI, and the APIs handle the fallback).</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-876">La classe <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSACng?displayProperty=nameWithType>, che fornisce un'implementazione CNG dell'algoritmo RSA.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-876">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSACng?displayProperty=nameWithType> class, which provides a CNG implementation of the RSA algorithm.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-877">Miglioramenti all'API RSA in modo che le azioni comuni non richiedano più il cast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-877">Enhancements to the RSA API so that common actions no longer require casting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-878">Ad esempio, la crittografia dei dati eseguita con un oggetto <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> richiede codice simile al seguente nelle versioni precedenti di .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-878">For example, encrypting data using an <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> object requires code like the following in previous versions of the .NET Framework.</span></span>

      [!code-csharp[WhatsNew.Casting#1](~/samples/snippets/csharp/VS_Snippets_CLR/whatsnew.casting/cs/program.cs#1)]
      [!code-vb[WhatsNew.Casting#1](~/samples/snippets/visualbasic/VS_Snippets_CLR/whatsnew.casting/vb/module1.vb#1)]

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-879">Il codice che usa le nuove API di crittografia in Framework .NET 4.6 può essere riscritto nel modo seguente per evitare il cast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-879">Code that uses the new cryptography APIs in .NET Framework 4.6 can be rewritten as follows to avoid the cast.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-880">**Supporto per la conversione di date e ore da o verso l'ora di Unix**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-880">**Support for converting dates and times to or from Unix time**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-881">Sono stati aggiunti i nuovi metodi seguenti alla struttura <xref:System.DateTimeOffset> per supportare la conversione di valori di data e ora da o verso l'ora di Unix:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-881">The following new methods have been added to the <xref:System.DateTimeOffset> structure to support converting date and time values to or from Unix time:</span></span>

    - <xref:System.DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeSeconds%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

    - <xref:System.DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeMilliseconds%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

    - <xref:System.DateTimeOffset.ToUnixTimeSeconds%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

    - <xref:System.DateTimeOffset.ToUnixTimeMilliseconds%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-882">**Opzioni di compatibilità**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-882">**Compatibility switches**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-883">La nuova classe <xref:System.AppContext> aggiunge una nuova funzione di compatibilità che consente agli autori di librerie di fornire agli utenti un meccanismo uniforme per la rinuncia esplicita alla nuova funzionalità,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-883">The new <xref:System.AppContext> class adds a new compatibility feature that enables library writers to provide a uniform opt-out mechanism for new functionality for their users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-884">che stabilisce un contratto a regime di controllo libero ("loosely-coupled") tra componenti per poter comunicare una richiesta di rinuncia esplicita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-884">It establishes a loosely-coupled contract between components in order to communicate an opt-out request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-885">Questa funzionalità è importante in genere quando viene apportata una modifica alle funzionalità esistenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-885">This capability is typically important when a change is made to existing functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-886">Al contrario, esiste già un consenso esplicito per la nuova funzionalità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-886">Conversely, there is already an implicit opt-in for new functionality.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-887">Con <xref:System.AppContext>, le librerie definiscono ed espongono le opzioni di compatibilità, mentre il codice che dipende dalle librerie può impostare tali opzioni in modo da influire sul comportamento della libreria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-887">With <xref:System.AppContext>, libraries define and expose compatibility switches, while code that depends on them can set those switches to affect the library behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-888">Per impostazione predefinita, le librerie forniscono la nuova funzionalità e la modificano (cioè offrono la funzionalità precedente) solo se l'opzione è impostata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-888">By default, libraries provide the new functionality, and they only alter it (that is, they provide the previous functionality) if the switch is set.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-889">Un'applicazione (o una libreria) può dichiarare il valore di un'opzione (che è sempre un valore <xref:System.Boolean>) definito da una libreria dipendente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-889">An application (or a library) can declare the value of a switch (which is always a <xref:System.Boolean> value) that a dependent library defines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-890">L'opzione è sempre implicitamente `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-890">The switch is always implicitly `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-891">Impostare l'opzione su `true` la abilita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-891">Setting the switch to `true` enables it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-892">Impostare in modo esplicito l'opzione su `false` fornisce il nuovo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-892">Explicitly setting the switch to `false` provides the new behavior.</span></span>

    ```csharp
    AppContext.SetSwitch("Switch.AmazingLib.ThrowOnException", true);
    ```

    ```vb
    AppContext.SetSwitch("Switch.AmazingLib.ThrowOnException", True)
    ```

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-893">La libreria deve controllare se un consumer è dichiarato il valore dell'opzione e si comporta in modo appropriato in base ad essa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-893">The library must check if a consumer has declared the value of the switch and then appropriately act on it.</span></span>

    ```csharp
    if (!AppContext.TryGetSwitch("Switch.AmazingLib.ThrowOnException", out shouldThrow))
    {
        // This is the case where the switch value was not set by the application.
        // The library can choose to get the value of shouldThrow by other means.
        // If no overrides nor default values are specified, the value should be 'false'.
        // A false value implies the latest behavior.
    }

    // The library can use the value of shouldThrow to throw exceptions or not.
    if (shouldThrow)
    {
        // old code
    }
    else
    {
        // new code
    }
    ```

    ```vb
    If Not AppContext.TryGetSwitch("Switch.AmazingLib.ThrowOnException", shouldThrow) Then
        ' This is the case where the switch value was not set by the application.
        ' The library can choose to get the value of shouldThrow by other means.
        ' If no overrides nor default values are specified, the value should be 'false'.
        ' A false value implies the latest behavior.
    End If

    ' The library can use the value of shouldThrow to throw exceptions or not.
    If shouldThrow Then
        ' old code
    Else
        ' new code
    End If
    ```

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-894">È opportuno usare un formato coerente per le opzioni, poiché si tratta di un contratto formale esposto da una libreria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-894">It's beneficial to use a consistent format for switches, since they are a formal contract exposed by a library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-895">Di seguito sono riportati due formati ovvi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-895">The following are two obvious formats.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-896">*Opzione*.*spaziodeinomi*.*nomeopzione*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-896">*Switch*.*namespace*.*switchname*</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-897">*Opzione*.*libreria*.*nomeopzione*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-897">*Switch*.*library*.*switchname*</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-898">**Modifiche apportate al modello asincrono basato su attività**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-898">**Changes to the task-based asynchronous pattern (TAP)**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-899">Per le app destinate a NET Framework 4.6, gli oggetti <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task> e <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task%601> ereditano le impostazioni cultura e le impostazioni cultura dell'interfaccia utente del thread chiamante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-899">For apps that target the .NET Framework 4.6, <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task> and <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task%601> objects inherit the culture and UI culture of the calling thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-900">Questo non incide sul comportamento delle app per versioni precedenti di .NET Framework o non destinate a una versione specifica di .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-900">The behavior of apps that target previous versions of the .NET Framework, or that do not target a specific version of the .NET Framework, is unaffected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-901">Per altre informazioni, vedere la sezione dedicata alle impostazioni cultura e alle operazioni asincrone basate su attività nell'argomento relativo alla classe <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-901">For more information, see the "Culture and task-based asynchronous operations" section of the <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> class topic.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-902">La classe <xref:System.Threading.AsyncLocal%601?displayProperty=nameWithType> consente di rappresentare i dati di ambiente locali rispetto a un flusso di controllo asincrono specificato, ad esempio un metodo `async`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-902">The <xref:System.Threading.AsyncLocal%601?displayProperty=nameWithType> class allows you to represent ambient data that is local to a given asynchronous control flow, such as an `async` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-903">Può essere usato per rendere persistenti i dati tra thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-903">It can be used to persist data across threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-904">È anche possibile definire un metodo di callback che riceve una notifica ogni volta che i dati di ambiente subiscono una modifica perché la proprietà <xref:System.Threading.AsyncLocal%601.Value%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> è stata modificata in modo esplicito oppure perché il thread ha rilevato una transizione di contesto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-904">You can also define a callback method that is notified whenever the ambient data changes either because the <xref:System.Threading.AsyncLocal%601.Value%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property was explicitly changed, or because the thread encountered a context transition.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-905">Tre metodi pratici, <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.CompletedTask%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.FromCanceled%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> e <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.FromException%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, sono stati aggiunti al modello asincrono basato su attività (TAP) per restituire le attività completate in un determinato stato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-905">Three convenience methods, <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.CompletedTask%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.FromCanceled%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, and <xref:System.Threading.Tasks.Task.FromException%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, have been added to the task-based asynchronous pattern (TAP) to return completed tasks in a particular state.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-906">La classe <xref:System.IO.Pipes.NamedPipeClientStream> ora supporta la comunicazione asincrona con il nuovo <xref:System.IO.Pipes.NamedPipeClientStream.ConnectAsync%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-906">The <xref:System.IO.Pipes.NamedPipeClientStream> class now supports asynchronous communication with its new <xref:System.IO.Pipes.NamedPipeClientStream.ConnectAsync%2A>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-907">ProcessOnStatus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-907">method.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-908">**EventSource supporta ora la scrittura nel registro eventi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-908">**EventSource now supports writing to the Event log**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-909">Ora è possibile usare la classe <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource> per registrare messaggi amministrativi o operativi nel registro eventi, oltre a tutte le sessioni ETW create nel computer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-909">You now can use the <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource> class to log administrative or operational messages to the event log, in addition to any existing ETW sessions created on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-910">In passato era necessario usare il pacchetto Microsoft.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource NuGet per questa funzionalità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-910">In the past, you had to use the Microsoft.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource NuGet package for this functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-911">Questa funzionalità è ora integrata in .NET Framework 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-911">This functionality is now built-into .NET Framework 4.6.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-912">Sia il pacchetto NuGet sia .NET Framework 4.6 sono stati aggiornati con le funzionalità seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-912">Both the NuGet package and .NET Framework 4.6 have been updated with the following features:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-913">**Eventi dinamici**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-913">**Dynamic events**</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-914">Consente eventi definiti al momento senza creare metodi di eventi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-914">Allows events defined "on the fly" without creating event methods.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-915">**Payload avanzati**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-915">**Rich payloads**</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-916">Consente di passare classi e matrici attribuite in modo specifico nonché tipi primitivi come un payload</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-916">Allows specially attributed classes and arrays as well as primitive types to be passed as a payload</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-917">**Rilevamento attività**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-917">**Activity tracking**</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-918">Comporta l'applicazione di tag di eventi tra gli eventi Start e Stop con un ID che rappresenta tutte le attività attualmente attive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-918">Causes Start and Stop events to tag events between them with an ID that represents all currently active activities.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-919">Per supportare queste funzionalità, il metodo <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.Write%2A> di overload è stato aggiunto alla classe <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-919">To support these features, the overloaded <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.Write%2A> method has been added to the <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-920">**Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-920">**Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-921">**Miglioramenti apportati a HDPI**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-921">**HDPI improvements**</span></span>
