    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-922">Il supporto di HDPI in WPF è stato migliorato in .NET Framework 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-922">HDPI support in WPF is now better in the .NET Framework 4.6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-923">Sono state apportate modifiche all'arrotondamento del layout per ridurre le istanze di ritaglio nei controlli con bordi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-923">Changes have been made to layout rounding to reduce instances of clipping in controls with borders.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-924">Per impostazione predefinita, questa funzionalità è abilitata solo se <xref:System.Runtime.Versioning.TargetFrameworkAttribute> è impostato su .NET 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-924">By default, this feature is enabled only if your <xref:System.Runtime.Versioning.TargetFrameworkAttribute> is set to .NET 4.6.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-925">Le applicazioni destinate alle versioni precedenti del framework, ma eseguite in .NET Framework 4.6, possono scegliere il nuovo comportamento aggiungendo la riga seguente alla sezione [\<runtime>](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/runtime-element.md) del file app.config:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-925">Applications that target earlier versions of the framework but are running on the .NET Framework 4.6 can opt in to the new behavior by adding the following line to the [\<runtime>](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/runtime-element.md) section of the app.config file:</span></span>

    ```xml
    <AppContextSwitchOverrides
    value="Switch.MS.Internal.DoNotApplyLayoutRoundingToMarginsAndBorderThickness=false"
    />
    ```

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-926">Le finestre WPF che si estendono su più monitor con impostazioni DPI diverse (configurazione di più DPI) sono ora visualizzate completamente senza aree nere.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-926">WPF windows straddling multiple monitors with different DPI settings (Multi-DPI setup) are now completely rendered without blacked-out regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-927">È possibile rifiutare esplicitamente questo comportamento disabilitandolo con l'aggiunta della riga seguente alla sezione `<appSettings>` del file di configurazione dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-927">You can opt out of this behavior by adding the following line to the `<appSettings>` section of the app.config file to disable this new behavior:</span></span>

    ```xml
    <add key="EnableMultiMonitorDisplayClipping" value="true"/>
    ```

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-928">Il supporto per il caricamento automatico del cursore appropriato in base all'impostazione DPI è stato aggiunto a <xref:System.Windows.Input.Cursor?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-928">Support for automatically loading the right cursor based on DPI setting has been added to  <xref:System.Windows.Input.Cursor?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-929">**Miglioramento della funzionalità touch**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-929">**Touch is better**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-930">I clienti hanno segnalato su [Connect](https://connect.microsoft.com/VisualStudio/feedback/details/903760/) che il comportamento imprevedibile della funzionalità touch è stato risolto in .NET Framework 4.6.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-930">Customer reports on [Connect](https://connect.microsoft.com/VisualStudio/feedback/details/903760/) that touch produces unpredictable behavior have been addressed in the .NET Framework 4.6.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-931">La soglia relativa al doppio tocco per le app di Windows Store e le applicazioni WPF ora è lo stesso in Windows 8.1 e versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-931">The double tap threshold for Windows Store applications and WPF applications is now the same in Windows 8.1 and above.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-932">**Supporto per finestre figlio trasparenti**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-932">**Transparent child window support**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-933">WPF in .NET Framework 4.6 supporta le finestre figlio trasparenti in Windows 8.1 e versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-933">WPF in the .NET Framework 4.6 supports transparent child windows in Windows 8.1 and above.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-934">Ciò consente di creare finestre figlio non rettangolari e trasparenti nelle finestre di primo livello.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-934">This allows you to create non-rectangular and transparent child windows in your top-level windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-935">È possibile abilitare questa funzionalità impostando la proprietà <xref:System.Windows.Interop.HwndSourceParameters.UsesPerPixelTransparency%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> su `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-935">You can enable this feature by setting the <xref:System.Windows.Interop.HwndSourceParameters.UsesPerPixelTransparency%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property to `true`.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-936">**Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-936">**Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-937">**Supporto di SSL**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-937">**SSL support**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-938">WCF ora supporta la versione SSL TLS 1.1 e TLS 1.2, oltre a SSL 3.0 e TLS 1.0, quando si usa NetTcp con la sicurezza del trasporto e l'autenticazione client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-938">WCF now supports SSL version TLS 1.1 and TLS 1.2, in addition to SSL 3.0 and TLS 1.0, when using NetTcp with transport security and client authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-939">Ora è possibile selezionare il protocollo da usare o disabilitare i protocolli precedenti, che sono meno sicuri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-939">It is now possible to select which protocol to use, or to disable old lesser secure protocols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-940">A tale scopo, è possibile impostare la proprietà <xref:System.ServiceModel.TcpTransportSecurity.SslProtocols%2A> o aggiungere il codice seguente a un file di configurazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-940">This can be done either by setting the <xref:System.ServiceModel.TcpTransportSecurity.SslProtocols%2A> property or by adding the following to a configuration file.</span></span>

    ```xml
    <netTcpBinding>
        <binding>
          <security mode= "None|Transport|Message|TransportWithMessageCredential" >
              <transport clientCredentialType="None|Windows|Certificate"
                        protectionLevel="None|Sign|EncryptAndSign"
                        sslProtocols="Ssl3|Tls1|Tls11|Tls12">
                </transport>
          </security>
        </binding>
    </netTcpBinding>
    ```

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-941">**Invio di messaggi tramite connessioni HTTP diverse**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-941">**Sending messages using different HTTP connections**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-942">WCF ora consente agli utenti di garantire l'invio di determinati messaggi usando diverse connessioni HTTP sottostanti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-942">WCF now allows users to ensure certain messages are sent using different underlying HTTP connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-943">Questo risultato può essere raggiunto in due modi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-943">There are two ways to do this:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-944">**Uso di un prefisso del nome del gruppo di connessione**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-944">**Using a connection group name prefix**</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-945">Gli utenti possono specificare una stringa che WCF userà come prefisso per il nome del gruppo di connessione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-945">Users can specify a string that WCF will use as a prefix for the connection group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-946">Due messaggi con prefissi diversi vengono inviati usando diverse connessioni HTTP sottostanti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-946">Two messages with different prefixes are sent using different underlying HTTP connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-947">Per impostare il prefisso, aggiungere una coppia chiave/valore alla proprietà <xref:System.ServiceModel.Channels.Message.Properties%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> del messaggio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-947">You set the prefix by adding a key/value pair to the message's <xref:System.ServiceModel.Channels.Message.Properties%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-948">La chiave è "HttpTransportConnectionGroupNamePrefix", mentre il valore è il prefisso desiderato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-948">The key is "HttpTransportConnectionGroupNamePrefix"; the value is the desired prefix.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-949">**Uso di channel factory diverse**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-949">**Using different channel factories**</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="80feb-950">Gli utenti possono anche attivare una funzionalità che assicura che i messaggi inviati con i canali creati da channel factory diverse useranno connessioni HTTP sottostanti diverse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-950">Users can also enable a feature that ensures that messages sent using channels created by different channel factories will use different underlying HTTP connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-951">Per abilitare questa funzionalità, gli utenti devono impostare `appSetting` su `true`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-951">To enable this feature, users must set the following `appSetting` to `true`:</span></span>

      ```xml
      <appSettings>
          <add key="wcf:httpTransportBinding:useUniqueConnectionPoolPerFactory" value="true" />
      </appSettings>
      ```

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-952">**Windows Workflow Foundation (WWF)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-952">**Windows Workflow Foundation (WWF)**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-953">Ora è possibile specificare il numero di secondi che un servizio di flusso di lavoro attenderà per una richiesta di operazione non ordinata quando esiste un segnalibro "non protocollo" in attesa prima del timeout della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-953">You can now specify the number of seconds a workflow service will hold on to an out-of-order operation request when there is an outstanding "non-protocol" bookmark before timing out the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-954">Un segnalibro "non protocollo" è un segnalibro che non è correlato alle attività di ricezione in attesa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-954">A "non-protocol" bookmark is a bookmark that is not related to outstanding Receive activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-955">Alcune attività creano segnalibri non protocollo all'interno della propria implementazione, quindi potrebbe non essere evidente che un segnalibro non protocollo esista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-955">Some activities create non-protocol bookmarks within their implementation, so it may not be obvious that a non-protocol bookmark exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-956">Sono incluse le attività relative allo stato e alla selezione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-956">These include State and Pick.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-957">Pertanto, se si ha un servizio del flusso di lavoro implementato con una macchina a stati o contenente un'attività di selezione, probabilmente si avranno segnalibri non protocollo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-957">So if you have a workflow service implemented with a state machine or containing a Pick activity, you will most likely have non-protocol bookmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-958">Specificare l'intervallo aggiungendo una riga simile alla seguente alla sezione `appSettings` del file di configurazione dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-958">You specify the interval by adding a line like the following to the `appSettings` section of your app.config file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <add key="microsoft:WorkflowServices:FilterResumeTimeoutInSeconds" value="60"/>
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-959">Il valore predefinito è 60 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-959">The default value is 60 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-960">Se `value` è impostato su 0, le richieste non ordinate vengono immediatamente rifiutate con un messaggio di errore simile al seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-960">If `value` is set to 0, out-of-order requests are immediately rejected with a fault with text that looks like this:</span></span>

  ```console
  Operation 'Request3|{http://tempuri.org/}IService' on service instance with identifier '2b0667b6-09c8-4093-9d02-f6c67d534292' cannot be performed at this time. Please ensure that the operations are performed in the correct order and that the binding in use provides ordered delivery guarantees.
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-961">Si tratta dello stesso messaggio che viene visualizzato se si riceve un messaggio di operazione non ordinato e non sono presenti segnalibri non protocollo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-961">This is the same message that you receive if an out-of-order operation message is received and there are no non-protocol bookmarks.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-962">Se il valore dell'elemento `FilterResumeTimeoutInSeconds` è diverso da zero, sono presenti segnalibri non protocollo, l'intervallo di timeout scade e l'operazione ha esito negativo con un messaggio di timeout.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-962">If the value of the `FilterResumeTimeoutInSeconds` element is non-zero, there are non-protocol bookmarks, and the timeout interval expires, the operation fails with a timeout message.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-963">**Transazioni**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-963">**Transactions**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-964">Ora è possibile includere l'identificatore di transazione distribuita per la transazione che ha generato un'eccezione derivata da <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionException>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-964">You can now include the distributed transaction identifier for the transaction that has caused an exception derived from <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionException> to be thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-965">A questo scopo, aggiungere la chiave seguente alla sezione `appSettings` del file di configurazione dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-965">You do this by adding the following key to the `appSettings` section of your app.config file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <add key="Transactions:IncludeDistributedTransactionIdInExceptionMessage" value="true"/>
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-966">Il valore predefinito è `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-966">The default value is `false`.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-967">**Servizi di rete**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-967">**Networking**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-968">**Riutilizzo di socket**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-968">**Socket reuse**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-969">Windows 10 include un nuovo algoritmo di rete ad alta scalabilità che consente di migliorare l'uso delle risorse del computer riutilizzando porte locali per le connessioni TCP in uscita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-969">Windows 10 includes a new high-scalability networking algorithm that makes better use of machine resources by reusing local ports for outbound TCP connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-970">.NET Framework 4.6 supporta il nuovo algoritmo, consentendo alle app .NET di sfruttare il nuovo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-970">.NET Framework 4.6 supports the new algorithm, enabling .NET apps to take advantage of the new behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-971">Nelle versioni precedenti di Windows era presente un limite di connessioni simultanee artificiali (in genere 16.384, la dimensione predefinita dell'intervallo di porte dinamiche), che poteva limitare la scalabilità di un servizio causando l'esaurimento delle porte quando sono sotto carico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-971">In previous versions of Windows, there was an artificial concurrent connection limit (typically 16,384, the default size of the dynamic port range), which could limit the scalability of a service by causing port exhaustion when under load.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-972">In .NET Framework 4.6 sono state aggiunte due nuove API per consentire il riutilizzo delle porte, che rimuove in modo efficace il limite di 64.000 sulle connessioni simultanee:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-972">In the .NET Framework 4.6, two new APIs have been added to enable port reuse, which effectively removes the 64K limit on concurrent connections:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-973">Il valore di enumerazione <xref:System.Net.Sockets.SocketOptionName?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-973">The <xref:System.Net.Sockets.SocketOptionName?displayProperty=nameWithType> enumeration value.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-974">Proprietà <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-974">The <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-975">Per impostazione predefinita, la proprietà <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> è `false`, a meno che il valore `HWRPortReuseOnSocketBind` della chiave del registro di sistema `HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\.NETFramework\v4.0.30319` sia impostato su 0x1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-975">By default, the <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property is `false` unless the `HWRPortReuseOnSocketBind` value of the `HKLM\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\.NETFramework\v4.0.30319` registry key is set to 0x1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-976">Per abilitare il riutilizzo delle porte locali su connessioni HTTP, impostare la proprietà <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> su `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-976">To enable local port reuse on HTTP connections, set the <xref:System.Net.ServicePointManager.ReusePort%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property to `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-977">In questo modo tutte le connessioni socket TCP in uscita da <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClient> e <xref:System.Net.HttpWebRequest> usano la nuova opzione di socket di Windows 10, [SO_REUSE_UNICASTPORT](/windows/desktop/WinSock/sol-socket-socket-options), che consente il riutilizzo delle porte locali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-977">This causes all outgoing TCP socket connections from <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClient> and <xref:System.Net.HttpWebRequest> to use a new Windows 10 socket option, [SO_REUSE_UNICASTPORT](/windows/desktop/WinSock/sol-socket-socket-options), that enables local port reuse.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-978">Gli sviluppatori che scrivono un'applicazione solo socket possono specificare l'opzione <xref:System.Net.Sockets.SocketOptionName?displayProperty=nameWithType> quando si chiama un metodo come <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket.SetSocketOption%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> in modo che i socket in uscita riutilizzino le porte locali durante l'associazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-978">Developers writing a sockets-only application can specify the <xref:System.Net.Sockets.SocketOptionName?displayProperty=nameWithType> option when calling a method such as <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket.SetSocketOption%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> so that outbound sockets reuse local ports during binding.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-979">**Supporto di nomi di dominio internazionali e di PunyCode**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-979">**Support for international domain names and PunyCode**</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="80feb-980">Una nuova proprietà, <xref:System.Uri.IdnHost%2A>, è stata aggiunta alla classe <xref:System.Uri> per migliorare il supporto dei nomi di dominio internazionali e di PunyCode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-980">A new property, <xref:System.Uri.IdnHost%2A>, has been added to the <xref:System.Uri> class to better support international domain names and PunyCode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-981">**Ridimensionamento nei controlli Windows Form**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-981">**Resizing in Windows Forms controls.**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-982">Questa funzionalità è stata estesa in .NET Framework 4.6 per includere i tipi <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DomainUpDown>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.NumericUpDown>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridViewComboBoxColumn>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridViewColumn> e <xref:System.Windows.Forms.ToolStripSplitButton>, nonché il rettangolo specificato dalla proprietà <xref:System.Drawing.Design.PaintValueEventArgs.Bounds%2A> usato per disegnare un oggetto <xref:System.Drawing.Design.UITypeEditor>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-982">This feature has been expanded in .NET Framework 4.6 to include the <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DomainUpDown>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.NumericUpDown>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridViewComboBoxColumn>, <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridViewColumn> and <xref:System.Windows.Forms.ToolStripSplitButton> types and the rectangle specified by the <xref:System.Drawing.Design.PaintValueEventArgs.Bounds%2A> property used when drawing a <xref:System.Drawing.Design.UITypeEditor>.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-983">È una funzionalità che prevede il consenso esplicito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-983">This is an opt-in feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-984">Per attivarla, impostare l'elemento `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` su `true` nel file di configurazione dell'applicazione (app.config):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-984">To enable it, set the `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` element to `true` in the application configuration (app.config) file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <appSettings>
      <add key="EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing" value="true" />
  </appSettings>
  ```

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-985">**Supporto per le codifiche della tabella codici**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-985">**Support for code page encodings**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-986">.NET Core supporta principalmente le codifiche Unicode e per impostazione predefinita offre un supporto limitato per le codifiche della tabella codici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-986">.NET Core primarily supports the Unicode encodings and by default provides limited support for code page encodings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-987">È possibile aggiungere il supporto delle codifiche della tabella codici disponibili in .NET Framework, ma non supportate in .NET Core registrando le codifiche della tabella codici con il metodo <xref:System.Text.Encoding.RegisterProvider%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-987">You can add support for code page encodings available in .NET Framework but unsupported in .NET Core by registering code page encodings with the <xref:System.Text.Encoding.RegisterProvider%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-988">Per ulteriori informazioni, vedere <xref:System.Text.CodePagesEncodingProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-988">For more information, see <xref:System.Text.CodePagesEncodingProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-989">**.NET Native**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-989">**.NET Native**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-990">Le app di Windows per Windows 10 destinate a .NET Core e scritte in C# o Visual Basic ora possono avvalersi di una nuova tecnologia che compila le app in codice nativo anziché IL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-990">Windows apps for Windows 10 that target .NET Core and are written in C# or Visual Basic can take advantage of a new technology that compiles apps to native code rather than IL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-991">Producono app caratterizzate da maggiore rapidità di avvio ed esecuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-991">They produce apps characterized by faster startup and execution times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-992">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Compilazione di app con .NET Native](../net-native/index.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-992">For more information, see [Compiling Apps with .NET Native](../net-native/index.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-993">Per una panoramica di .NET Native che esamina le differenze rispetto alla compilazione JIT e NGEN e descrive tutti i vantaggi per il codice, vedere [Compilazione e .NET Native](../net-native/net-native-and-compilation.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-993">For an overview of .NET Native that examines how it differs from both JIT compilation and NGEN and what that means for your code, see [.NET Native and Compilation](../net-native/net-native-and-compilation.md).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-994">Le app vengono compilate in codice nativo per impostazione predefinita quando si compilano con Visual Studio 2015 o versione successiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-994">Your apps are compiled to native code by default when you compile them with Visual Studio 2015 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-995">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Introduzione a .NET Native](../net-native/getting-started-with-net-native.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-995">For more information, see [Getting Started with .NET Native](../net-native/getting-started-with-net-native.md).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-996">Per supportare il debug di app .NET Native, è stata aggiunta una serie di nuove interfacce ed enumerazioni all'API di debug non gestito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-996">To support debugging .NET Native apps, a number of new interfaces and enumerations have been added to the unmanaged debugging API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-997">Per altre informazioni, vedere l'argomento [Debug (riferimenti alle API non gestite)](../unmanaged-api/debugging/index.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-997">For more information, see the [Debugging (Unmanaged API Reference)](../unmanaged-api/debugging/index.md) topic.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-998">**Pacchetti .NET Framework open source**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-998">**Open-source .NET Framework packages**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-999">I pacchetti .NET Core come le raccolte non modificabili, le [API SIMD](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.Bcl.Simd) e le API di rete come quelle presenti nello spazio dei nomi <xref:System.Net.Http> sono ora disponibili come pacchetti open source su [GitHub](https://github.com/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-999">.NET Core packages such as the immutable collections, [SIMD APIs](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.Bcl.Simd), and networking APIs such as those found in the <xref:System.Net.Http> namespace are now available as open source packages on [GitHub](https://github.com/).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1000">Per accedere al codice, vedere [.NET su GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1000">To access the code, see [.NET on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1001">Per altre informazioni e indicazioni su come contribuire a questi pacchetti, vedere [Componenti di base e open source di .NET](../get-started/net-core-and-open-source.md) e la [home page di .NET su GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/home).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1001">For more information and how to contribute to these packages, see [.NET Core and Open-Source](../get-started/net-core-and-open-source.md), [.NET Home Page on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/home).</span></span>

<a name="v452" />

## <a name="whats-new-in-net-framework-452"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-1002">Novità di .NET Framework 4.5.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1002">What's new in .NET Framework 4.5.2</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1003">**Nuove API per app ASP.NET**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1003">**New APIs for ASP.NET apps.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1004">I nuovi metodi <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.AddOnSendingHeaders%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> e <xref:System.Web.HttpResponseBase.AddOnSendingHeaders%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> consentono di esaminare e modificare le intestazioni di risposta e il codice di stato mentre la risposta viene scaricata sull'app client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1004">The new <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.AddOnSendingHeaders%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Web.HttpResponseBase.AddOnSendingHeaders%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you inspect and modify response headers and status code as the response is being flushed to the client app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1005">Considerare l'uso di questi metodi invece degli eventi <xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.PreSendRequestHeaders> e <xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.PreSendRequestContent>, poiché sono più efficienti e affidabili.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1005">Consider using these methods instead of the <xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.PreSendRequestHeaders> and <xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.PreSendRequestContent> events; they are more efficient and reliable.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1006">Il metodo <xref:System.Web.Hosting.HostingEnvironment.QueueBackgroundWorkItem%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> consente di pianificare piccoli elementi di lavoro in background.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1006">The <xref:System.Web.Hosting.HostingEnvironment.QueueBackgroundWorkItem%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method lets you schedule small background work items.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1007">ASP.NET tiene traccia di questi elementi e impedisce a IIS di chiudere improvvisamente il processo di lavoro finché non saranno stati completati tutti gli elementi di lavoro in background.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1007">ASP.NET tracks these items and prevents IIS from abruptly terminating the worker process until all background work items have completed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1008">Non è possibile chiamare questo metodo all'esterno del dominio dell'app gestita di ASP.NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1008">This method can't be called outside an ASP.NET managed app domain.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1009">Le nuove proprietà <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.HeadersWritten?displayProperty=nameWithType> e <xref:System.Web.HttpResponseBase.HeadersWritten?displayProperty=nameWithType> restituiscono valori booleani che indicano che le intestazioni di risposta sono state scritte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1009">The new <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.HeadersWritten?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Web.HttpResponseBase.HeadersWritten?displayProperty=nameWithType> properties return Boolean values that indicate whether the response headers have been written.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1010">È possibile usare queste proprietà per accertarsi che le chiamate alle API come <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.StatusCode%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> (che genera eccezioni se le intestazioni sono state scritte) abbiano esito positivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1010">You can use these properties to make sure that calls to APIs such as <xref:System.Web.HttpResponse.StatusCode%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> (which throw exceptions if the headers have been written) will succeed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1011">**Ridimensionamento nei controlli Windows Form**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1011">**Resizing in Windows Forms controls.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1012">Questa funzionalità è stata ampliata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1012">This feature has been expanded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1013">È ora possibile usare l'impostazione DPI di sistema per ridimensionare i componenti dei seguenti controlli aggiuntivi (ad esempio, la freccia a discesa nelle caselle combinate):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1013">You can now use the system DPI setting to resize components of the following additional controls (for example, the drop-down arrow in combo boxes):</span></span>

  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.ComboBox>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.ToolStripComboBox>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.ToolStripMenuItem>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.Cursor>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridView>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridViewComboBoxColumn>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1014">È una funzionalità che prevede il consenso esplicito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1014">This is an opt-in feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1015">Per attivarla, impostare l'elemento `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` su `true` nel file di configurazione dell'applicazione (app.config):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1015">To enable it, set the `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` element to `true` in the application configuration (app.config) file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <appSettings>
      <add key="EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing" value="true" />
  </appSettings>
  ```

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1016">**Nuova funzionalità per il flusso di lavoro**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1016">**New workflow feature.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1017">Una funzionalità di gestione risorse che usa il metodo <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A> (e che quindi implementa l'interfaccia <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification>) può usare il nuovo metodo <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoteAndEnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> per richiedere quanto segue:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1017">A resource manager that's using the <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A> method (and therefore implementing the <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> interface) can use the new <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoteAndEnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method to request the following:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1018">Promozione della transazione in transazione MSDTC (Microsoft Distributed Transaction Coordinator).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1018">Promote the transaction to a Microsoft Distributed Transaction Coordinator (MSDTC) transaction.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1019">Sostituire <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> con una<xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification>, cioè un'integrazione durevole che supporta i commit monofase.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1019">Replace <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> with an <xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification>, which is a durable enlistment that supports single phase commits.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1020">È possibile eseguire questa operazione nello stesso dominio dell'app; inoltre, non è necessario altro codice non gestito che interagisca con MSDTC per eseguire la promozione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1020">This can be done within the same app domain, and doesn't require any extra unmanaged code to interact with MSDTC to perform the promotion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1021">Questo nuovo metodo può essere chiamato solo quando esiste una chiamata in attesa da <xref:System.Transactions?displayProperty=nameWithType> al metodo <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> di `Promote` implementata dall'integrazione promuovibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1021">The new method can be called only when there's an outstanding call from <xref:System.Transactions?displayProperty=nameWithType> to the <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification>`Promote` method that's implemented by the promotable enlistment.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1022">**Miglioramenti apportati alla profilatura**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1022">**Profiling improvements.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1023">Le seguenti nuove API di profilatura non gestite offrono funzioni di profilatura più solide:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1023">The following new unmanaged profiling APIs provide more robust profiling:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1024">Struttura COR_PRF_ASSEMBLY_REFERENCE_INFO</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1024">COR_PRF_ASSEMBLY_REFERENCE_INFO Structure</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/cor-prf-assembly-reference-info-structure.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1025">Enumerazione COR_PRF_HIGH_MONITOR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1025">COR_PRF_HIGH_MONITOR Enumeration</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/cor-prf-high-monitor-enumeration.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1026">Metodo GetAssemblyReferences</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1026">GetAssemblyReferences Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilercallback6-getassemblyreferences-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1027">Metodo GetEventMask2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1027">GetEventMask2 Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo5-geteventmask2-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1028">Metodo SetEventMask2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1028">SetEventMask2 Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerinfo5-seteventmask2-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1029">Metodo AddAssemblyReference</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1029">AddAssemblyReference Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/profiling/icorprofilerassemblyreferenceprovider-addassemblyreference-method.md)

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1030">Le precedenti implementazioni di `ICorProfiler` supportavano il caricamento differito degli assembly dipendenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1030">Previous `ICorProfiler` implementations supported lazy loading of dependent assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1031">Le nuove API di profilatura richiedono assembly dipendenti inseriti dal profiler per il caricamento immediato, invece di essere caricato dopo la completa inizializzazione dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1031">The new profiling APIs require dependent assemblies that are injected by the profiler to be loadable immediately, instead of being loaded after the app is fully initialized.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1032">Questa modifica non incide sugli utenti delle API `ICorProfiler` esistenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1032">This change doesn't affect users of the existing `ICorProfiler` APIs.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1033">**Miglioramenti apportati al debug**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1033">**Debugging improvements.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1034">Le seguenti nuove API di debug non gestite offrono una migliore integrazione con un profiler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1034">The following new unmanaged debugging APIs provide better integration with a profiler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1035">È ora possibile accedere ai metadati inseriti dal profiler oltre alle variabili e al codice locali prodotti dalle richieste ReJIT del compilatore durante il debug di dump.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1035">You can now access metadata inserted by the profiler as well as local variables and code produced by compiler ReJIT requests when dump debugging.</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1036">Metodo SetWriteableMetadataUpdateMode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1036">SetWriteableMetadataUpdateMode Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugprocess7-setwriteablemetadataupdatemode-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1037">Metodo EnumerateLocalVariablesEx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1037">EnumerateLocalVariablesEx Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugilframe4-enumeratelocalvariablesex-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1038">Metodo GetLocalVariableEx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1038">GetLocalVariableEx Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugilframe4-getlocalvariableex-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1039">Metodo GetCodeEx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1039">GetCodeEx Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugilframe4-getcodeex-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1040">Metodo GetActiveReJitRequestILCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1040">GetActiveReJitRequestILCode Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugfunction3-getactiverejitrequestilcode-method.md)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1041">Metodo GetInstrumentedILMap</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1041">GetInstrumentedILMap Method</span></span>](../unmanaged-api/debugging/icordebugilcode2-getinstrumentedilmap-method.md)

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1042">**Modifiche apportate alla traccia eventi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1042">**Event tracing changes.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1043">.NET Framework 4.5.2 consente di eseguire attività out-of-process basate su Event Tracing for Windows (ETW) per una superficie di attacco maggiore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1043">.NET Framework 4.5.2 enables out-of-process, Event Tracing for Windows (ETW)-based activity tracing for a larger surface area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1044">Ciò consente ai fornitori di Advanced Power Management (APM) di offrire strumenti semplici che tengono accuratamente traccia dei costi delle singole richieste e attività cross-thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1044">This enables Advanced Power Management (APM) vendors to provide lightweight tools that accurately track the costs of individual requests and activities that cross threads.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1045">Questi eventi vengono generati solo quando sono abilitati dai controller ETW; di conseguenza, le modifiche non influiscono sul codice ETW scritto in precedenza oppure sul codice eseguito con ETW disattivato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1045">These events are raised only when ETW controllers enable them; therefore, the changes don't affect previously written ETW code or code that runs with ETW disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1046">**Promozione di una transazione e relativa conversione in integrazione durevole**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1046">**Promoting a transaction and converting it to a durable enlistment**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1047"><xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoteAndEnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> è una nuova API aggiunta a .NET Framework 4.5.2 e 4.6:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1047"><xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.PromoteAndEnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> is a new API added to .NET Framework 4.5.2 and 4.6:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  [System.Security.Permissions.PermissionSetAttribute(System.Security.Permissions.SecurityAction.LinkDemand, Name = "FullTrust")]
  public Enlistment PromoteAndEnlistDurable(Guid resourceManagerIdentifier,
                                            IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification promotableNotification,
                                            ISinglePhaseNotification enlistmentNotification,
                                            EnlistmentOptions enlistmentOptions)
  ```

  ```vb
  <System.Security.Permissions.PermissionSetAttribute(System.Security.Permissions.SecurityAction.LinkDemand, Name:="FullTrust")>
  public Function PromoteAndEnlistDurable(resourceManagerIdentifier As Guid,
                                          promotableNotification As IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification,
                                          enlistmentNotification As ISinglePhaseNotification,
                                          enlistmentOptions As EnlistmentOptions) As Enlistment
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1048">Il metodo può essere usato da un elenco creato in precedenza da <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> in risposta al metodo <xref:System.Transactions.ITransactionPromoter.Promote%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1048">The method may be used by an enlistment that was previously created by <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistPromotableSinglePhase%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> in response to the <xref:System.Transactions.ITransactionPromoter.Promote%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1049">Chiede a `System.Transactions` di alzare la transazione al livello di transazione MSDTC e di "convertire" l'elenco promuovibile in un elenco durevole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1049">It asks `System.Transactions` to promote the transaction to an MSDTC transaction and to "convert" the promotable enlistment to a durable enlistment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1050">Dopo il completamento di questo metodo, l'interfaccia <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> non sarà più usata come riferimento da `System.Transactions` e le eventuali notifiche future arriveranno all'interfaccia <xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification> fornita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1050">After this method completes successfully, the <xref:System.Transactions.IPromotableSinglePhaseNotification> interface will no longer be referenced by `System.Transactions`, and any future notifications will arrive on the provided <xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1051">L'elenco in questione deve agire come un elenco durevole, supportando la registrazione e il ripristino delle transazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1051">The enlistment in question must act as a durable enlistment, supporting transaction logging and recovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1052">Vedere <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> per informazioni dettagliate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1052">Refer to <xref:System.Transactions.Transaction.EnlistDurable%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> for details.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1053">Inoltre, l'elenco deve supportare <xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1053">In addition, the enlistment must support <xref:System.Transactions.ISinglePhaseNotification>.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1054">Questo metodo può essere chiamato *solo* durante l'elaborazione di una chiamata <xref:System.Transactions.ITransactionPromoter.Promote%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1054">This method can *only* be called while processing an <xref:System.Transactions.ITransactionPromoter.Promote%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1055">Diversamente, viene generata un'eccezione <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionException>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1055">If that is not the case, a <xref:System.Transactions.TransactionException> exception is thrown.</span></span>

<a name="v451" />

## <a name="whats-new-in-net-framework-451"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-1056">Novità di .NET Framework 4.5.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1056">What's new in .NET Framework 4.5.1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1057">**Aggiornamenti di aprile 2014**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1057">**April 2014 updates**:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1058">[Visual Studio 2013 Update 2](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=393658) include alcuni aggiornamenti ai modelli di libreria di classi portabile per supportare questi scenari:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1058">[Visual Studio 2013 Update 2](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=393658) includes updates to the Portable Class Library templates to support these scenarios:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1059">È possibile usare le API di Windows Runtime in librerie portabili destinate a Windows 8.1, Windows Phone 8.1 e Windows Phone Silverlight 8.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1059">You can use Windows Runtime APIs in portable libraries that target Windows 8.1, Windows Phone 8.1, and Windows Phone Silverlight 8.1.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1060">È possibile includere XAML (tipi Windows.UI.XAML) nelle librerie portabili quando la destinazione è Windows 8.1 o Windows Phone 8.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1060">You can include XAML (Windows.UI.XAML types) in portable libraries when you target Windows 8.1 or Windows Phone 8.1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1061">Sono supportati i modelli XAML seguenti: Pagina vuota, Dizionario risorse, Controllo basato su modelli e Controllo utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1061">The following XAML templates are supported:  Blank Page, Resource Dictionary, Templated Control, and User Control.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1062">È possibile creare una componente Windows Runtime portabile (.winmd file) da usare in app di Windows Store destinate a Windows 8.1 e Windows Phone 8.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1062">You can create a portable Windows Runtime component (.winmd file) for use in Store apps that target Windows 8.1 and Windows Phone 8.1.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1063">È possibile cambiare associazione a una libreria di classi Windows Store o Windows Phone Store come una Libreria di classi portabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1063">You can retarget a Windows Store or Windows Phone Store class library like a Portable Class Library.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1064">Per altre informazioni su queste modifiche, vedere [Libreria di classi portabile](../../standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1064">For more information about these changes, see [Portable Class Library](../../standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1065">Il set di contenuti di .NET Framework ora include la documentazione relativa a .NET Native, una tecnologia di precompilazione per la creazione e la distribuzione di app di Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1065">The .NET Framework content set now includes documentation for .NET Native, which is a precompilation technology for building and deploying Windows apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1066">.NET Native compila le app direttamente in codice nativo piuttosto che in linguaggio intermedio (IL), per ottenere migliori prestazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1066">.NET Native compiles your apps directly to native code, rather than to intermediate language (IL), for better performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1067">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere [Compilazione di app con .NET Native](../net-native/index.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1067">For details, see [Compiling Apps with .NET Native](../net-native/index.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1068">[Reference Source per .NET Framework](https://referencesource.microsoft.com/) offre una nuova esperienza di esplorazione e funzionalità migliorate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1068">The [.NET Framework Reference Source](https://referencesource.microsoft.com/) provides a new browsing experience and enhanced functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1069">È ora possibile esplorare il codice sorgente di .NET Framework online, [scaricare i riferimenti](https://referencesource.microsoft.com/download.html) per la visualizzazione offline ed eseguire le origini (inclusi aggiornamenti e patch) durante il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1069">You can now browse through the .NET Framework source code online, [download the reference](https://referencesource.microsoft.com/download.html) for offline viewing, and step through the sources (including patches and updates) during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1070">Per altre informazioni, vedere il post di blog relativo al [nuovo aspetto di Reference Source per .NET](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/a-new-look-for-net-reference-source/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1070">For more information, see the blog entry [A new look for .NET Reference Source](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/a-new-look-for-net-reference-source/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1071">Le nuove funzionalità e i miglioramenti nelle classi di base di .NET Framework 4.5.1 includono:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1071">New features and enhancements in the base classes in .NET Framework 4.5.1 include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1072">Reindirizzamento di associazione automatico per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1072">Automatic binding redirection for assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1073">A partire da Visual Studio 2013, quando si compila un'app destinata a .NET Framework 4.5.1, è possibile aggiungere reindirizzamenti di associazione al file di configurazione dell'app se quest'ultima o i relativi componenti fanno riferimento a più versioni dello stesso assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1073">Starting with Visual Studio 2013, when you compile an app that targets the .NET Framework 4.5.1, binding redirects may be added to the app configuration file if your app or its components reference multiple versions of the same assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1074">È inoltre possibile abilitare questa funzionalità per i progetti destinati a versioni precedenti di .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1074">You can also enable this feature for projects that target older versions of the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1075">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Procedura: abilitare e disabilitare il reindirizzamento di associazione automatico](../configure-apps/how-to-enable-and-disable-automatic-binding-redirection.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1075">For more information, see [How to: Enable and Disable Automatic Binding Redirection](../configure-apps/how-to-enable-and-disable-automatic-binding-redirection.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1076">Possibilità di raccogliere informazioni di diagnostica che consentono agli sviluppatori di migliorare le prestazioni delle applicazioni server e cloud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1076">Ability to collect diagnostics information to help developers improve the performance of server and cloud applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1077">Per altre informazioni, vedere i metodi <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.WriteEventWithRelatedActivityId%2A> e <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.WriteEventWithRelatedActivityIdCore%2A> nella classe <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1077">For more information, see the <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.WriteEventWithRelatedActivityId%2A> and <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource.WriteEventWithRelatedActivityIdCore%2A> methods in the <xref:System.Diagnostics.Tracing.EventSource> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1078">Capacità di compattare in modo esplicito gli heap di oggetti grandi durante la Garbage Collection.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1078">Ability to explicitly compact the large object heap (LOH) during garbage collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1079">Per altre informazioni, vedere la proprietà <xref:System.Runtime.GCSettings.LargeObjectHeapCompactionMode%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1079">For more information, see the <xref:System.Runtime.GCSettings.LargeObjectHeapCompactionMode%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1080">Altri miglioramenti alle prestazioni, quali la sospensione di app ASP.NET, i miglioramenti JIT multicore e un avvio più rapido delle app in seguito a un aggiornamento di .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1080">Additional performance improvements such as ASP.NET app suspension, multi-core JIT improvements, and faster app startup after a .NET Framework update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1081">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere l'[annuncio di .NET Framework 4.5.1](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/) e il post di blog sulla [sospensione di app ASP.NET](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/asp-net-app-suspend-responsive-shared-net-web-hosting/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1081">For details, see the [.NET Framework 4.5.1 announcement](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/) and the [ASP.NET app suspend](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/asp-net-app-suspend-responsive-shared-net-web-hosting/) blog post.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1082">I miglioramenti di Windows Form includono:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1082">Improvements to Windows Forms include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1083">Ridimensionamento nei controlli Windows Form.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1083">Resizing in Windows Forms controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1084">È possibile usare l'impostazione DPI per ridimensionare i componenti dei controlli (ad esempio, le icone visualizzate in una griglia delle proprietà) scegliendo una voce nel file di configurazione dell'applicazione (app.config) relativo alla propria app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1084">You can use the system DPI setting to resize components of controls (for example, the icons that appear in a property grid) by opting in with an entry in the application configuration file (app.config) for your app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1085">Questa funzionalità è attualmente supportata nei seguenti controlli Windows Form:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1085">This feature is currently supported in the following Windows Forms controls:</span></span>

  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.PropertyGrid>
  - <xref:System.Windows.Forms.TreeView>
  - <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1086">Alcuni aspetti di <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridView> (per gli altri controlli supportati, vedere le [nuove funzionalità nella versione 4.5.2](#v452))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1086">Some aspects of the <xref:System.Windows.Forms.DataGridView> (see [new features in 4.5.2](#v452) for additional controls supported)</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1087">Per attivare questa funzionalità, aggiungere un nuovo elemento \<appSettings> al file di configurazione (app.config) e impostare l'elemento `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` su `true`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1087">To enable this feature, add a new \<appSettings> element to the configuration file (app.config) and set the `EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing` element to `true`:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <appSettings>
      <add key="EnableWindowsFormsHighDpiAutoResizing" value="true" />
  </appSettings>
  ```

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1088">I miglioramenti durante il debug delle app .NET Framework in Visual Studio 2013 includono:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1088">Improvements when debugging your .NET Framework apps in Visual Studio 2013 include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1089">Valori restituiti nel debugger di Visual Studio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1089">Return values in the Visual Studio debugger.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1090">Quando si esegue il debug di un'app gestita in Visual Studio 2013, nella finestra Auto vengono restituiti tipi e valori per i metodi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1090">When you debug a managed app in Visual Studio 2013, the Autos window displays return types and values for methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1091">Queste informazioni sono disponibili per applicazioni desktop, Windows Store e Windows Phone.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1091">This information is available for desktop, Windows Store, and Windows Phone apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1092">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Esaminare i valori restituiti dalle chiamate di metodo](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/visualstudio/visual-studio-2013/dn323257(v=vs.120)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1092">For more information, see [Examine return values of method calls](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/visualstudio/visual-studio-2013/dn323257(v=vs.120)).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1093">Modifica e continua per app a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1093">Edit and Continue for 64-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1094">In Visual Studio 2013 è supportata la funzionalità Modifica e continuazione per le applicazioni gestite a 64 bit per desktop, Windows Store e Windows Phone.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1094">Visual Studio 2013 supports the Edit and Continue feature for 64-bit managed apps for desktop, Windows Store, and Windows Phone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1095">Le limitazioni esistenti restano valide per le app a 32 bit e a 64 bit. Vedere l'ultima sezione dell'articolo [Modifiche al codice supportate (C#)](/visualstudio/debugger/supported-code-changes-csharp).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1095">The existing limitations remain in effect for both 32-bit and 64-bit apps (see the last section of the [Supported Code Changes (C#)](/visualstudio/debugger/supported-code-changes-csharp) article).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1096">Debug asincrono.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1096">Async-aware debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1097">Per semplificare il debug delle app asincrone in Visual Studio 2013, lo stack di chiamate nasconde il codice dell'infrastruttura fornito dai compilatori per supportare la programmazione asincrona e inoltre si concatena nei frame padre logici, in modo da poter seguire più chiaramente l'esecuzione logica del programma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1097">To make it easier to debug asynchronous apps in Visual Studio 2013, the call stack hides the infrastructure code provided by compilers to support asynchronous programming, and also chains in logical parent frames so you can follow logical program execution more clearly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1098">La finestra Attività in parallelo è stata sostituita da una finestra Attività, contenente le attività correlate a uno specifico punto di interruzione e qualsiasi altra attività attualmente attiva o pianificata nell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1098">A Tasks window replaces the Parallel Tasks window and displays tasks that relate to a particular breakpoint, and also displays any other tasks that are currently active or scheduled in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1099">Informazioni su questa funzionalità sono disponibili nella sezione relativa al debug asincrono nell'[annuncio di .NET Framework 4.5.1](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1099">You can read about this feature in the "Async-aware debugging" section of the [.NET Framework 4.5.1 announcement](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1100">Supporto avanzato delle eccezioni per i componenti Windows Runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1100">Better exception support for Windows Runtime components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1101">In Windows 8.1 le eccezioni generate dalle app di Windows Store conservano le informazioni sull'errore che ha generato l'eccezione, anche oltre i limiti di linguaggio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1101">In Windows 8.1, exceptions that arise from Windows Store apps preserve information about the error that caused the exception, even across language boundaries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1102">Informazioni su questa funzionalità sono disponibili nella sezione relativa allo sviluppo di app di Windows Store nell'[annuncio di .NET Framework 4.5.1](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1102">You can read about this feature in the "Windows Store app development" section of the [.NET Framework 4.5.1 announcement](https://devblogs.microsoft.com/dotnet/announcing-the-net-framework-4-5-1-preview/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1103">A partire da Visual Studio 2013, è possibile usare lo strumento [Mpgo.exe (Managed Profile Guided Optimization)](../tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md) per ottimizzare le app di Windows 8.x Store e quelle desktop.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1103">Starting with Visual Studio 2013, you can use the [Managed Profile Guided Optimization Tool (Mpgo.exe)](../tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md) to optimize Windows 8.x Store apps as well as desktop apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="80feb-1104">Per le nuove funzionalità in ASP.NET 4.5.1, vedere [Note sulla versione di ASP.NET and Web Tools per Visual Studio 2013](/aspnet/visual-studio/overview/2013/release-notes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1104">For new features in ASP.NET 4.5.1, see [ASP.NET and Web Tools for Visual Studio 2013 Release Notes](/aspnet/visual-studio/overview/2013/release-notes).</span></span>

<a name="v45" />

## <a name="whats-new-in-net-framework-45"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-1105">Novità di .NET Framework 4.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1105">What's new in .NET Framework 4.5</span></span>

### <a name="base-classes"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-1106">Classi di base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1106">Base classes</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1107">Possibilità di ridurre i riavvii di sistema rilevando e chiudendo le applicazioni .NET Framework 4 durante la distribuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1107">Ability to reduce system restarts by detecting and closing .NET Framework 4 applications during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1108">Vedere [Riduzione dei riavvii del sistema durante le installazioni di .NET Framework 4.5](../deployment/reducing-system-restarts.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1108">See [Reducing System Restarts During .NET Framework 4.5 Installations](../deployment/reducing-system-restarts.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1109">Supporto per le matrici di dimensioni maggiori di 2 GB nelle piattaforme a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1109">Support for arrays that are larger than 2 gigabytes (GB) on 64-bit platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1110">Questa funzionalità può essere abilitata nel file di configurazione dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1110">This feature can be enabled in the application configuration file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1111">Vedere l'[\<elemento gcAllowVeryLargeObjects>](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/gcallowverylargeobjects-element.md), che elenca anche altre restrizioni per le dimensioni di oggetti e matrici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1111">See the [\<gcAllowVeryLargeObjects> element](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/gcallowverylargeobjects-element.md), which also lists other restrictions on object size and array size.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1112">Miglioramento delle prestazioni tramite Garbage Collection in background per server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1112">Better performance through background garbage collection for servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1113">Se si usa la funzionalità di Garbage Collection del server in .NET Framework 4.5, verrà automaticamente abilità la Garbage Collection in background.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1113">When you use server garbage collection in the .NET Framework 4.5, background garbage collection is automatically enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1114">Vedere la sezione "Operazione di Garbage Collection in background per server" nell'argomento [Principi fondamentali di Garbage Collection](../../standard/garbage-collection/fundamentals.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1114">See the Background Server Garbage Collection section of the [Fundamentals of Garbage Collection](../../standard/garbage-collection/fundamentals.md) topic.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1115">Compilazione JIT in background, eventualmente disponibile nei processori multicore per migliorare le prestazioni delle applicazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1115">Background just-in-time (JIT) compilation, which is optionally available on multi-core processors to improve application performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1116">Vedere <xref:System.Runtime.ProfileOptimization>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1116">See <xref:System.Runtime.ProfileOptimization>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1117">Possibilità di limitare il tempo durante il quale il motore delle espressioni regolari tenterà di risolvere un'espressione regolare prima del timeout. Vedere la proprietà <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex.MatchTimeout%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1117">Ability to limit how long the regular expression engine will attempt to resolve a regular expression before it times out. See the <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex.MatchTimeout%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1118">Possibilità di definire le impostazioni cultura predefinite per un dominio di applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1118">Ability to define the default culture for an application domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1119">Vedere la classe <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1119">See the <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1120">Supporto della console per la codifica Unicode (UTF-16).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1120">Console support for Unicode (UTF-16) encoding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1121">Vedere la classe <xref:System.Console>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1121">See the <xref:System.Console> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1122">Supporto per il controllo delle versioni dei dati di confronto e ordinamento delle stringhe di impostazioni cultura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1122">Support for versioning of cultural string ordering and comparison data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1123">Vedere la classe <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1123">See the <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1124">Miglioramento delle prestazioni in fase di recupero di risorse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1124">Better performance when retrieving resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1125">Vedere [Creazione del pacchetto e distribuzione delle risorse in applicazioni desktop](../resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1125">See [Packaging and Deploying Resources](../resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md).</span></span>

### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="80feb-1183">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1183">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1191">Possibilità di controllare se il contesto dei dati per un contenitore di elementi è disconnesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1191">Ability to check whether the data context for an item container is disconnected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1192">Possibilità di impostare la quantità di tempo che deve trascorrere tra le modifiche alle proprietà e gli aggiornamenti delle origini dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1192">Ability to set the amount of time that should elapse between property changes and data source updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1193">Supporto avanzato per l'implementazione di modelli di eventi deboli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1193">Improved support for implementing weak event patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="80feb-1194">Inoltre, gli eventi possono ora accettare estensioni di markup.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="80feb-1194">Also, events can now accept markup extensions.</span></span>
